<span class="plumedtooltip">LABEL<span class="right">a label for the action so that its output can be referenced in the input to other actions<i></i></span></span>=<b name="data/plumed/md/cry_disp.datq" onclick='showPath("data/plumed/md/cry_disp.dat","data/plumed/md/cry_disp.datq","data/plumed/md/cry_disp.datq","black")'>q</b><span style="display:none;" id="data/plumed/md/cry_disp.datq">The CONTACTMAP action with label <b>q</b> calculates the following quantities:<table  align="center" frame="void" width="95%" cellpadding="5%"><tr><td width="5%"><b> Quantity </b>  </td><td width="5%"><b> Type </b>  </td><td><b> Description </b> </td></tr><tr><td width="5%">q</td><td width="5%"><font color="black">scalar</font></td><td>the sum of all the switching function on all the distances</td></tr></table></span>
<span class="plumedtooltip">SUM<span class="right"> calculate the sum of all the contacts in the input<i></i></span></span>
<span class="plumedtooltip">NOPBC<span class="right"> ignore the periodic boundary conditions when calculating distances<i></i></span></span>
